North / Kimberley Newell \nTier 2 Weekend Tickets from £127 + booking fee \nChild Tickets from £5 + booking fee \nWhat started as a birthday BBQ with a couple of DJs and a handful of friends, has become the perfect summer escape for festival-goers, offering renowned and upcoming acts, interactive art installations, immersive theatre, comedy, a fancy dress parade, the annual dog show, a huge family programme for kids of all ages and of course its own heated outdoor swimming pool. \nStandon Calling is renowned for its eclectic musical line-up and 2015 will be no different. The Dandy Warhols will be exclusive to Standon this summer, playing the best of their 20-year Indie reign. Masterful dance band Little Dragon will be gracing the stage with an electrifying performance, whilst Roots Manuva brings UK Hip Hop and roots to the fields.  \nHouse and disco comes courtesy of New Yorker Andy Butler and his ever-changing Hercules & Love Affair, while Nottingham's own Saint Raymond brings a helping of folk rock to the fields. Supporting rising stars, Standon welcomes BRIT winner and Rudimental collaborator Ella Eyre, BBC Sound of 2015 rock duo Slaves, dreamy electronic dance trio Real Lies, hotly tipped soulful crooner Kwabs, Liverpool trio All We Are and more.   \nWe promise you a weekend to remember right through to the Sunday night when Basement Jaxx bring the curtain down with on our 10th birthday party celebrations. \nWhatever you’re looking for in a festival, Standon Calling is the overgrown house party where all revelers come together. By day, choose between relaxing in the Lordship gardens or exploring our ever-expanding programme of music, immersive theatre and interactive workshops. By night, dance until 5am in our myriad of late night venues, or hunt down our late night bill in the woods.   \nJoin us as we celebrate Standon Calling’s 10th birthday in the stunning grounds of Standon Lordship for the perfect mix of music, partying and a healthy dose of unexpected surprises! \n\n \nAll Weekend Tickets include camping.\n \nCampervan Tickets must be purchased in addition to Weekend Tickets.\n \nCampervan Power Hook-Ups must be purchased in addition to Campervan Tickets. \n \nTiered Tickets System\nThe Tiered Tickets System means that the earlier you buy, the cheaper the ticket. Super Early Bird Tickets are our cheapest and are each year available right after the festival ends. Once these have sold out, the prices rise a little to the next level which is regular Early Bird Tickets. Once these have sold out we go to Tier 1. This method rewards those who buy early and helps to balance supply and demand for our tickets. \n \nTERMS AND CONDITIONS \nTickets are non-refundable except if the festival is cancelled, Standon Calling has been negligent or acted in breach of contract. However, refunds will not be given if the event is cancelled due to any of the following reasons: terrorism, biological action, foot and mouth, the aliens land, data problems, SARS, national mourning, avian flu, swine flu, or you forget what weekend it’s on. If you are under 18 you will only be granted admission to the event if accompanied by a guardian who is over 21.
